# atl command reference

This file is generated by `scripts/gen-docs.sh` from the clap command tree. Do not edit by hand.

## atl

Unified CLI for Atlassian Confluence and Jira

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

**Subcommands**

- `confluence` тАФ Confluence operations
- `jira` тАФ Jira operations
- `init` тАФ Initialize configuration file
- `config` тАФ Manage configuration profiles
- `completions` тАФ Generate shell completion scripts
- `self` тАФ Manage the atl binary itself (check/update)
- `api` тАФ Make an authenticated REST request against Confluence or Jira
- `browse` тАФ Open a Confluence page or Jira issue in the default browser
- `alias` тАФ Manage user-defined command aliases
- `auth` тАФ Manage authentication тАФ login, logout, status, token

### atl confluence

Confluence operations

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

**Subcommands**

- `read` тАФ Read a page by ID
- `info` тАФ Get page metadata
- `search` тАФ Search pages with CQL
- `space` тАФ List spaces
- `children` тАФ List child pages
- `create` тАФ Create a new page
- `update` тАФ Update an existing page
- `delete` тАФ Delete a page
- `attachment` тАФ Attachment operations
- `find` тАФ Find pages by title
- `export` тАФ Export a page with attachments to a local directory
- `copy-tree` тАФ Copy a page tree to another space/parent
- `property` тАФ Content property operations
- `label` тАФ Label management
- `blog` тАФ Blog post management
- `versions` тАФ Page version history
- `version-detail` тАФ Get a specific page version
- `likes` тАФ Page likes
- `operations` тАФ Page operations/permissions
- `ancestors` тАФ Page ancestors
- `descendants` тАФ Page descendants
- `footer-comment` тАФ Footer comment management (v2)
- `inline-comment` тАФ Inline comment management (v2)
- `whiteboard` тАФ Whiteboard management
- `database` тАФ Database management
- `folder` тАФ Folder management
- `custom-content` тАФ Custom content management
- `task` тАФ Task management
- `admin-key` тАФ Admin key management
- `classification` тАФ Content classification management
- `user` тАФ Confluence user operations
- `convert-ids` тАФ Convert content IDs between formats
- `app-property` тАФ App property management
- `page-list` тАФ List pages (v2)
- `update-title` тАФ Update page title only
- `likes-count` тАФ Get like count for a page
- `likes-users` тАФ Get users who liked a page
- `page-custom-content` тАФ List custom content in a page
- `redact` тАФ Redact content from a page

#### atl confluence read

Read a page by ID

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence read [OPTIONS] <PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<PAGE_ID>` тАФ Page ID
- `--body-format` тАФ Body format
- `--include-labels` тАФ Include labels in the response
- `--include-properties` тАФ Include properties in the response
- `--include-operations` тАФ Include operations in the response
- `--include-versions` тАФ Include version details in the response
- `--include-collaborators` тАФ Include collaborators in the response
- `--include-favorited-by` тАФ Include favorited-by info in the response
- `--web` тАФ Open the page in a browser instead of printing
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence space role [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

**Subcommands**

- `list` тАФ List roles for a space
- `get` тАФ Get a role by ID
- `create` тАФ Create a role
- `update` тАФ Update a role
- `delete` тАФ Delete a role
- `mode` тАФ Get space roles mode

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)

#### atl confluence create

Create a new page

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence create [OPTIONS] --title <TITLE> --body <BODY>
```

**Options**

- `--space, -s` тАФ Space key (resolved to ID internally)
- `--space-id` тАФ Space ID (numeric, skips key-to-ID lookup)
- `--title, -t` тАФ Page title
- `--body, -b` тАФ Page body. Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--parent` тАФ Parent page ID
- `--input-format` тАФ Input format for the body
- `--private` тАФ Create as a private (personal) page
- `--subtype` тАФ Page subtype (e.g. "page", "blog")
- `--embedded` тАФ Create as embedded content
- `--root-level` тАФ Create at root level (no parent)
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

- `--body, -b` тАФ New body. Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--input-format` тАФ Input format for the body
- `--version-message` тАФ Version comment/message
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use

- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager

#### atl confluence attachment

Attachment operations

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence attachment [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use

- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output

- `list` тАФ List attachments for a page
- `get` тАФ Get attachment by ID (v2)
- `upload` тАФ Upload an attachment to a page
- `delete` тАФ Delete an attachment
- `download` тАФ Download an attachment
- `labels` тАФ List attachment labels (v2)
- `comments` тАФ List attachment comments (v2)
- `operations` тАФ Attachment operations (v2)
- `versions` тАФ Attachment version history (v2)
- `version-details` тАФ Get specific attachment version details (v2)
- `property` тАФ Attachment property management (v2)

##### atl confluence attachment list

List attachments for a page

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence attachment list [OPTIONS] <PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<PAGE_ID>` тАФ Page ID
- `--limit, -l` тАФ Max results
- `--pattern` тАФ Glob pattern to filter attachment filenames (e.g. "*.pdf")
- `--media-type` тАФ Filter by media type (e.g. "image/png", "application/pdf")
- `--filename` тАФ Filter by filename
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output

#### atl confluence find

#### atl confluence copy-tree

Copy a page tree to another space/parent

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence copy-tree [OPTIONS] <SOURCE_PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<SOURCE_PAGE_ID>` тАФ Source page ID (root of the tree to copy)
- `--target-space` тАФ Target space key (resolved to ID internally)
- `--target-space-id` тАФ Target space ID (numeric, skips key-to-ID lookup)
- `--target-parent` тАФ Target parent page ID
- `--depth, -d` тАФ Maximum depth to copy (0 = source page only)
- `--dry-run` тАФ Show what would be copied without making changes
- `--exclude` тАФ Glob pattern to exclude pages by title
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

##### atl confluence inline-comment create

Create an inline comment

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence inline-comment create [OPTIONS] --body <BODY> --inline-marker-ref <INLINE_MARKER_REF> <PAGE_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<PAGE_ID>` тАФ Page ID
- `--body, -b` тАФ Comment body (storage format). Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--inline-marker-ref` тАФ Inline marker reference (from the page content)
- `--text-selection` тАФ Text selection to highlight
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

- `--template-key` тАФ Template key (for whiteboards)

- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

##### atl confluence task get

Get a task by ID

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence task get [OPTIONS] <TASK_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<TASK_ID>` тАФ Task ID
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

##### atl confluence task update

Update a task (e.g. mark complete/incomplete)

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence task update [OPTIONS] --status <STATUS> <TASK_ID>
```

**Options**

- `<TASK_ID>` тАФ Task ID
- `--status` тАФ New status (complete, incomplete)
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

#### atl confluence classification

Content classification management

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence classification [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

**Subcommands**

- `list` тАФ List classification levels
- `get-page` тАФ Get classification for a page
- `set-page` тАФ Set classification for a page
- `reset-page` тАФ Reset classification for a page
- `get-blogpost` тАФ Get classification for a blog post
- `set-blogpost` тАФ Set classification for a blog post
- `reset-blogpost` тАФ Reset classification for a blog post
- `get-space` тАФ Get classification for a space
- `set-space` тАФ Set classification for a space
- `reset-space` тАФ Reset classification for a space
- `get-database` тАФ Get classification for a database
- `set-database` тАФ Set classification for a database
- `reset-database` тАФ Reset classification for a database
- `get-whiteboard` тАФ Get classification for a whiteboard
- `set-whiteboard` тАФ Set classification for a whiteboard
- `reset-whiteboard` тАФ Reset classification for a whiteboard

**Subcommands**

- `list` тАФ List app properties (operates on the calling app's properties)
- `get` тАФ Get an app property
- `set` тАФ Set an app property
- `delete` тАФ Delete an app property

##### atl confluence app-property list

List app properties (operates on the calling app's properties)

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl confluence app-property list [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

### atl jira

Jira operations

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

**Subcommands**

- `search` тАФ Search issues with JQL
- `view` тАФ View an issue
- `create` тАФ Create a new issue
- `update` тАФ Update an issue
- `delete` тАФ Delete an issue
- `move` тАФ Transition an issue to another status
- `assign` тАФ Assign an issue
- `comment` тАФ Add a comment to an issue
- `comments` тАФ List comments for an issue
- `comment-get` тАФ Get a specific comment
- `comment-delete` тАФ Delete a comment
- `transitions` тАФ List available transitions for an issue
- `project` тАФ Project management
- `board` тАФ Board management
- `sprint` тАФ Sprint management
- `backlog-move` тАФ Move issues to backlog
- `me` тАФ Show current user info
- `epic` тАФ Epic management
- `link` тАФ Link two issues
- `link-type` тАФ Issue link type management
- `issue-link-get` тАФ Get an issue link by ID
- `issue-link-delete` тАФ Delete an issue link by ID
- `remote-link` тАФ Add a remote link to an issue
- `remote-links` тАФ List remote links for an issue
- `remote-link-delete` тАФ Delete a remote link
- `clone` тАФ Clone an issue
- `worklog` тАФ Worklog management
- `filter` тАФ Saved filter management
- `attach` тАФ Attach a file to an issue
- `watch` тАФ Watch an issue
- `unwatch` тАФ Unwatch an issue
- `watchers` тАФ List watchers for an issue
- `vote` тАФ Vote for an issue
- `unvote` тАФ Remove your vote from an issue
- `changelog` тАФ View issue changelog (history of changes)
- `component` тАФ Component management
- `version` тАФ Version management
- `dashboard` тАФ Dashboard management
- `field` тАФ Field management
- `user` тАФ User operations
- `group` тАФ Group management
- `notify` тАФ Send a notification about an issue
- `create-meta` тАФ Get issue creation metadata
- `edit-meta` тАФ Get issue edit metadata
- `issue-type` тАФ Issue type management
- `priority` тАФ Priority management
- `resolution` тАФ Resolution management
- `status` тАФ Status management
- `screen` тАФ Screen management
- `workflow` тАФ Workflow management
- `workflow-scheme` тАФ Workflow scheme management
- `permission-scheme` тАФ Permission scheme management
- `notification-scheme` тАФ Notification scheme management
- `issue-security-scheme` тАФ Issue security scheme management
- `field-config` тАФ Field configuration management
- `issue-type-scheme` тАФ Issue type scheme management
- `role` тАФ Standalone role management
- `banner` тАФ Announcement banner
- `configuration` тАФ View system configuration
- `task` тАФ Async task management
- `attachment` тАФ Attachment administration
- `project-category` тАФ Project category management
- `server-info` тАФ Show server information
- `webhook` тАФ Webhook management
- `audit-records` тАФ View audit records
- `permissions` тАФ List all permissions
- `my-permissions` тАФ List my permissions
- `labels` тАФ List all labels
- `bulk-create` тАФ Bulk create issues from a JSON array
- `archive` тАФ Archive one or more issues
- `unarchive` тАФ Unarchive one or more issues

#### atl jira search

Search issues with JQL

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira search [OPTIONS] [JQL]
```

**Options**

- `<JQL>` тАФ JQL query (combined with filter flags via AND)
- `--limit, -l` тАФ Max results per page
- `--all` тАФ Fetch all results (auto-paginate)
- `--fields, -f` тАФ Fields to return (comma-separated)
- `--status` тАФ Filter by status name (e.g. "Open", "In Progress")
- `--priority` тАФ Filter by priority name
- `--assignee` тАФ Filter by assignee (account ID or "currentUser()")
- `--reporter` тАФ Filter by reporter
- `--type` тАФ Filter by issue type (e.g. Bug, Task, Story)
- `--label` тАФ Filter by label
- `--component` тАФ Filter by component
- `--resolution` тАФ Filter by resolution
- `--created` тАФ Filter: created on or after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--created-after` тАФ Filter: created after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--updated` тАФ Filter: updated on or after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--updated-after` тАФ Filter: updated after date (YYYY-MM-DD)
- `--watching` тАФ Only issues you are watching
- `--order-by` тАФ Order results by field (e.g. "created", "priority")
- `--reverse` тАФ Reverse sort order (use with --order-by)
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

#### atl jira view

View an issue

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira view [OPTIONS] <KEY>
```

**Options**

- `<KEY>` тАФ Issue key (e.g. PROJ-123)
- `--web` тАФ Open the issue in a browser instead of printing
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output

- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

#### atl jira create

Create a new issue

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira create [OPTIONS] --project <PROJECT> --issue-type <ISSUE_TYPE> --summary <SUMMARY>
```

**Options**

- `--project` тАФ Project key
- `--issue-type, -t` тАФ Issue type (e.g. Task, Bug, Story)
- `--summary, -s` тАФ Summary
- `--description, -d` тАФ Description
- `--assignee` тАФ Assignee account ID
- `--priority` тАФ Priority name
- `--labels` тАФ Labels (comma-separated)
- `--parent` тАФ Parent issue key (for subtasks)
- `--fix-version` тАФ Fix version(s), comma-separated
- `--component` тАФ Component(s), comma-separated
- `--custom` тАФ Custom field (repeatable), e.g. --custom customfield_10001=value
- `--input-format` тАФ Input format for the body
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

- `--assignee` тАФ New assignee account ID

- `--component` тАФ Component(s), comma-separated

- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors

- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output

- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output

- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

**Subcommands**

- `get` тАФ Get epic details
- `issues` тАФ List issues in an epic
- `add` тАФ Move issues into an epic
- `remove` тАФ Remove issues from their epic

```
Usage: atl jira filter delete [OPTIONS] <ID>
```

- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output

- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

#### atl jira notify

Send a notification about an issue

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl jira notify [OPTIONS] --subject <SUBJECT> --body <BODY> <KEY>
```

**Options**

- `<KEY>` тАФ Issue key (e.g. PROJ-123)
- `--subject, -s` тАФ Notification subject
- `--body, -b` тАФ Notification body. Use @file to read from file, or - for stdin
- `--to` тАФ Recipient account IDs (repeatable)
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format

- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

### atl api

Make an authenticated REST request against Confluence or Jira

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl api [OPTIONS] --service <SERVICE> <ENDPOINT>
```

**Options**

- `<ENDPOINT>` тАФ REST endpoint path (e.g. `rest/api/2/myself`). Leading slash optional
- `--service` тАФ Which Atlassian product to target
- `--method, -X` тАФ HTTP method (default: GET)
- `--header, -H` тАФ Custom header in the form `KEY:VALUE`. Repeatable
- `--field, -f` тАФ String field in the JSON body, `KEY=VALUE`. `VALUE` may be `@file` to read the contents of a file, or `-` to read stdin. Repeatable. Mutually exclusive with `--input`
- `--raw-field` тАФ Raw JSON field in the JSON body, `KEY=VALUE`. `VALUE` is parsed as JSON (e.g. `--raw-field count=42`, `--raw-field tags=[1,2,3]`). Repeatable. Mutually exclusive with `--input`. No short form because `-F` is reserved for `--format`
- `--input` тАФ Read the request body verbatim from a file, or `-` for stdin. Mutually exclusive with `--field` / `--raw-field`
- `--query` тАФ Query parameter in the form `KEY=VALUE`. Repeatable. No short form because `-q` is reserved for `--quiet`
- `--paginate` тАФ Auto-follow pagination until the server reports no more pages
- `--preview` тАФ Print the constructed request to stderr and exit without sending
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

### atl browse

Open a Confluence page or Jira issue in the default browser

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl browse [OPTIONS] <TARGET>
```

**Options**

- `<TARGET>` тАФ Page ID or Jira issue key to open in a browser
- `--service` тАФ Which service to target
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use

#### atl alias set

Create or update an alias

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl alias set [OPTIONS] <NAME> <EXPANSION>
```

**Options**

- `<NAME>` тАФ Alias name (invoked as `atl <name>`)
- `<EXPANSION>` тАФ Expansion. Supports shell-style quoting, e.g. `'jira search "project=FOO"'`
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

#### atl alias list

List all configured aliases

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl alias list [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

### atl auth

Manage authentication тАФ login, logout, status, token

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl auth [OPTIONS] <COMMAND>
```

**Options**

- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--profile, -p` тАФ Profile name to use
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

**Subcommands**

- `login` тАФ Log in to Confluence or Jira and store the token in the OS keyring
- `logout` тАФ Remove stored credentials for a profile/service
- `status` тАФ Show which profiles/services are authenticated
- `token` тАФ Print the resolved API token to stdout

#### atl auth login

Log in to Confluence or Jira and store the token in the OS keyring

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl auth login [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--service` тАФ Service to log in to (defaults to both)
- `--profile` тАФ Profile name (overrides the global --profile for this login)
- `--domain` тАФ Atlassian domain (e.g. acme.atlassian.net). Prompted when omitted
- `--email` тАФ Email address for Basic auth. Prompted when omitted and --auth-type=basic
- `--auth-type` тАФ Authentication mechanism (basic = email + API token, bearer = PAT)
- `--with-token` тАФ Read the token from stdin instead of prompting interactively
- `--skip-verify` тАФ Skip the live verification request against the Atlassian API
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

#### atl auth logout

Remove stored credentials for a profile/service

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl auth logout [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--service` тАФ Service to log out of (defaults to both)
- `--profile` тАФ Profile name (overrides the global --profile for this logout)
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

#### atl auth status

Show which profiles/services are authenticated

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl auth status [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--profile` тАФ Show status for this profile only (defaults to all)
- `--skip-verify` тАФ Skip the live verification request against the Atlassian API
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)

#### atl auth token

Print the resolved API token to stdout

**Usage**

```
Usage: atl auth token [OPTIONS]
```

**Options**

- `--service` тАФ Which service's token to print (required)
- `--profile` тАФ Profile name (overrides the global --profile)
- `--force` тАФ Print the token even when stdout is a TTY
- `--verbose, -v` тАФ Increase logging verbosity (-v, -vv, -vvv)
- `--quiet, -q` тАФ Suppress all output except errors
- `--config` тАФ Path to configuration file
- `--format, -F` тАФ Output format
- `--no-color` тАФ Disable colored output
- `--no-pager` тАФ Do not pipe long output through a pager
- `--jq` тАФ Query output with a jq expression
- `--template` тАФ Format output with a minijinja template
- `--retries` тАФ Maximum HTTP retries on transient errors (0 = off)
